      let client2 = window.AmeyoClient.init();

      var requestBody = JSON.stringify({
        "statsName": 'QueueCallsStatsT24D24'        
      });

      var requestObject = {
        url: "ameyorestapi/stats/getAllStats",
        headers: {
            "content-type": "application/json"
        },
        method: "POST",
        body: requestBody
    };
    try{
        client2.httpRequest.invokeAmeyo(requestObject).then(function(responseData) {
          console.log(responseData);
        });
    }catch(e){            
        console.log("DashboardApp: Could not fetch queueCall Stats",e)
    }
